	1675978556	amb_disaster_volcano			\ev_amb\on_map\disasters\amb_disaster_volcano	"volcano" schematic. Uses it's own animation state machine. Each animation state triggers the corresponding switch state in colcano_loop actor. (Note that "Start" is just silence, and transitions straight away to "Idle") Oneshots are handled via separate OS event (as should be timed with animation, e.g., explosion)  This event and the switch used was designed for volcano_eruption_state_machine, which could cycle between different states, return too and from idle/eruption/cooldown/etc.  However, this has since been replaced with volcano_eruption_always_state_machine, which follows more of a linear progression, and cannot swap back and forth between states.  We're opting to keep the wwise setup should this be changed in the future (allowing us to tweak triggers fairly easily and still get representative audio output from state changes).  Currently, switch groups are triggered on... start - default switch group on emitter in schematic idle - triggered confusingly on "buildup" state eruption - on "erutpion" (with the oneshot on timeline - should probably be changed to vfx trigger, but up until the methods are changed we're stuck with this) cooldown - beginning of "cooldown" state idle (again) - partway through "cooldown" state end - end of "cooldown" state (as we have no animation to trigger on default end state   In case we need to rollback to old Entity usage, the asset can still be found here: \game\main_menu\gfx\models\mapitems\weather\volcano\_volcano_weather_entities.asset
